SUBENT        14329001   20130820                             13931432900100001 
BIB                 15         72                                 1432900100002 
TITLE      Neutron Spectra Emitted by 239Pu, 238U, 235U, Pb, Nb,  1432900100003 
           Ni, Al and C Irradiated by 14 MeV Neutrons             1432900100004 
AUTHOR     (J.L.Kammerdiener)                                     1432900100005 
INSTITUTE  (1USADAV)                                              1432900100006 
REFERENCE  (R,UCRL-51232,1972) Ph.D.thesis                        1432900100007 
REL-REF    (O,10423001,L.F.Hansen+,P,USNDC-9,84,197311), Ni data. 1432900100008 
           (O,V1004001,T.Kawano,W,KAWANO,2013)                    1432900100009 
             Angle-integrated spectra derived from present        1432900100010 
             experiment                                           1432900100011 
FACILITY   (ICTR,1USALRL) Insulated core transformer accelerator. 1432900100012 
INC-SOURCE (D-T) Deuteron on tritium                              1432900100013 
DETECTOR   (SCIN,GLASD) NE-213 scintillator, 6Li glass detector.  1432900100014 
PART-DET   (N,G)                                                  1432900100015 
METHOD     (TOF,PSD,RINGR) Time of flight, pulse shape            1432900100016 
           discrimination allowed both neutron and gamma          1432900100017 
           measurements. High-energy runs (1-15 MeV) were         1432900100018 
           measured with NE-213 scintillator and low energy runs  1432900100019 
            (below 1 MeV) were measured with the glass detector.  1432900100020 
           Ring geometry.                                         1432900100021 
ANALYSIS   (REDUC) The entire data reduction process was          1432900100022 
           computerized. The RAW output facilitated generation    1432900100023 
           of input to the one step data reduction code RING,     1432900100024 
           written especially for ring geometry time-of-flight    1432900100025 
           data reduction. Each data set was normalized to a      1432900100026 
           ninety degree ring position. The time-of-arrival of    1432900100027 
           each energy was calculated from the source-ring        1432900100028 
           flight time plus the ring-detector flight time.        1432900100029 
CORRECTION The data were corrected for effects due to impurities, 1432900100030 
           multiple scattering and absorption; the corrections    1432900100031 
           were made in one step using SORS-MSC, a Monte Carlo    1432900100032 
           neutron transport code. The SCRS code was extensively  1432900100033 
           modified by David Cummings for the purpose of making   1432900100034 
           multiple scattering corrections. The multiple          1432900100035 
           scattering theory employed was that of Parker and      1432900100036 
           Amster.                                                1432900100037 
ERR-ANALYS (DATA-ERR) Data which has been corrected for multiple  1432900100038 
           scattering and attenuation have been plotted with the  1432900100039 
           combined errors of experimental counting statistics    1432900100040 
           and the computed standard deviation of the Monte Carlo 1432900100041 
           methods used in computing corrections. The             1432900100042 
           experimental statistical error is taken as the square  1432900100043 
           root of the number of counts in the interval           1432900100044 
           indicated. Statistical errors have been kept small in  1432900100045 
           most cases, since counting statistics were good. In    1432900100046 
           almost all cases, counting statistics are less than    1432900100047 
           10%. Systematic uncertainties dominate. The primary    1432900100048 
           systematic error is the uncertainty in the detector    1432900100049 
           efficiency. There is a known systematic uncertainty    1432900100050 
           resulting from finite experimental time and energy     1432900100051 
           resolution; the resulting uncertainty in quoted energy 1432900100052 
           of the emitted neutron causes resolvable energy levels 1432900100053 
           to have an unnatural width which is characteristic of  1432900100054 
           the energy resolution at that energy.                  1432900100055 
           (ERR-S,,10.0) less than 10%.                           1432900100056 
COMMENT    From conversation of M.B. Chadwick with John           1432900100057 
           Kammerdiener: the final data are the "line",           1432900100058 
            not the symbols (as the symbols are only every 10th   1432900100059 
           point). The "corrected" data accounts for multiple     1432900100060 
           scattering in the target, etc. The symbols are         1432900100061 
           plotted every 10th point and only mark the line. The   1432900100062 
           data are probably available on a PDP-8 punched paper   1432900100063 
           tape. A few extra points: 1) Carbon data cannot be     1432900100064 
           extracted from the Fig.41. 2) 239Pu data needs more    1432900100065 
           analysis and users should take absolute cross section  1432900100066 
           values with reservations. Thesis says his 239pu data   1432900100067 
           is contaminated, or rather, is 239Pu and 56Fe from     1432900100068 
           the stainless steel casing. Finally, help of S.        1432900100069 
           Mashnik (LANL) with proper data interpretation was     1432900100070 
           essential for this compilation.                        1432900100071 
HISTORY    (20121207C) BP                                         1432900100072 
           (20130712A) BP added reference to Los Alamos estimate  1432900100073 
           by T. Kawano.                                          1432900100074
